                function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
                    var regExp = new RegExp(cookieName + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
                    var matches = document.cookie.match(regExp);
                    return matches ? matches[1] : null;
                }

                function getUserDataFromCookie() {
                    var geoMetaTag = document.querySelector('meta[name="geolocation-detected"]');
                    var data = {
                        id: getCookieValue(window.HS_CONFIG.cookieIdentifierUserId),
                        country: getCookieValue(window.HS_CONFIG.cookieIdentifierCountry),
                        logged_in: getCookieValue(window.HS_CONFIG.cookieIdentifierLoggedIn) === '1',
                        geo_detected_country: geoMetaTag ? geoMetaTag.content : null,
                    };
                    return data;
                }

                window.dataLayer.push({
                    environment: window.HS_CONFIG.environment,
                    frontend_service: window.HS_CONFIG.frontendService,
                    user: getUserDataFromCookie(),
                    is_post: false,
                    is_frontpage: true,
                });

                // helper to integrate A/B test
                window._galleryTest = {
                    onUpdate: [],
                    variant: false,
                    update: function (variant) {
                        this.variant = variant;
                        while (this.onUpdate.length) {
                            this.onUpdate.shift()();
                        }
                    },
                    setOnUpdate: function (onUpdateCallback) {
                        if (this.variant) {
                            onUpdateCallback();
                        } else {
                            this.onUpdate.push(onUpdateCallback);
                        }
                    }
                };

                window.delayedScriptLoader = {
                    GDPR_PRISTINE: 0,
                    GDPR_ACCEPTED: 1,
                    GDPR_REJECTED: 2,
                    GDPR_REJECTED_TWICE: 3,
                    pending_scripts: [],
                    should_load_immediately: function () {
                        return true;
                        if (this.immediate_load == undefined) {
                            var gdprCookie = document.cookie.match(/hs-gdpr-optin15022019v2=(.+?)(?=\b)/);
                            var gdprCookieValue = gdprCookie ? parseInt(gdprCookie[1]) : 0
                            var isSubjectToGDPR = document.querySelector('meta[name=gdpr-subject]');

                            this.immediate_load = gdprCookieValue == this.GDPR_ACCEPTED || !isSubjectToGDPR;
                        }
                        return this.immediate_load;
                    },
                    register_script: function (script) {
                        if (this.should_load_immediately()) {
                            script();
                        } else {
                            this.pending_scripts.push(script);
                        }
                    },
                    load_pending_scripts: function () {
                        while (this.pending_scripts.length) {
                            var currentScript = this.pending_scripts[0];

                            try {
                                currentScript();
                            } catch (e) {
                                console.warn("Failed to load delayed script");
                            }

                            this.pending_scripts.shift(0, 1);
                        }

                        this.immediate_load = true;
                        console.warn("Scripts will load immediately from now!");
                    }
                };
                // helper to integrate interactive story scripts
                window.appReady = {
                    loaded: false,
                    environment: {},
                    listeners: [],
                    add: function (listener) {
                        if (this.loaded) {
                            listener(this.environment);
                        } else {
                            this.listeners.push(listener);
                        }
                    },
                    call: function (environment) {
                        this.environment = environment;
                        while (this.listeners.length > 0) {
                            this.listeners[0](this.environment);
                            this.listeners.splice(0, 1);
                        }
                        this.loaded = true;
                    }
                };

   var googletag = googletag || {};
	googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

	function getUrlParameter(name) {
		name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
		var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
		var results = regex.exec(location.search);
		return results === null ? null : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
	};

	function addCampaignIdToDataLayer(data) {
		if(data.campaignId) {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				'hsCampaignId': data.campaignId
			});
		}
	}

	var customTargetingValue = getUrlParameter('preview_id');

	window._nativeAdListener = {
		_queue: {},
		addData: function(frameId, slotData) {
			if (this._queue[frameId] !== undefined) {
				return this._queue[frameId].onReceive(slotData);
			}

			this._addToQueue(frameId, { data: slotData });
		},
		addListener: function(frameId, onReceive) {
			if (this._queue[frameId] !== undefined) {
				return onReceive(this._queue[frameId].data);
			}

			this._addToQueue(frameId, { onReceive: onReceive });
		},
		_addToQueue: function(frameId, obj) {
			this._queue[frameId] = obj;
		}
	};

	window._defineAndDisplayNewAdSlot = function(slotName, type, opts) {
		opts.onRenderEnded = opts.onRenderEnded || function() {};
		opts.onSlot = opts.onSlot || function() {};

		var adPosition = getAdPosition(type);
		if (!adPosition) return;

		window.adPositions[slotName] = adPosition;
		var adSlot = window.adPositions[slotName]['anyViewport'] || window.adPositions[slotName][window.adViewport];
		
		var renderEnded = adSlot.renderEnded || function() {};

		googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
			if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === slotName) {
				renderEnded(event);
				opts.onRenderEnded(event);
			}
		});

		var slot = window._defineAdSlot(adSlot, slotName);
		opts.onSlot(slot);

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.display(slotName);
			window._ad_slots[slotName] = slot;
		});
	};

	function _onRenderLeaderboardTop(data) {
		var leaderboardTop = document.getElementById('leaderboard-top');
		if (data.isEmpty) {
			leaderboardTop.classList.add('empty');
			return;
		}

		var width = data.size[0];
		var height = data.size[1];
		var isFullWidth = (width === 2400 && height === 600);
		
		// set to correct sizes after ad is loaded
		var leaderboardTopIframe = leaderboardTop.querySelector('iframe');
		if (leaderboardTopIframe !== null) {
			leaderboardTopIframe.height = height;
			leaderboardTopIframe.width = width;
		}

		if (isFullWidth) {
			var vpWidth = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientWidth, window.innerWidth || 0);
			var ratio = height / width;
			var scaledAdHeight = vpWidth * ratio;
			leaderboardTopIframe.height = Math.round(scaledAdHeight);
			leaderboardTop.style.paddingTop = '0';
			leaderboardTop.style.paddingBottom = '0';
		} else {
			leaderboardTop.style.minHeight = height + 'px';
		}
	}

	function getAdPosition(id) {
		if (window.adPositions && typeof window.adPositions[id] === "undefined") {
			console.error(id, 'is not defined yet')	;
			return null;
		}

		return window.adPositions[id];
	}

	function shouldLeaderboardTopBeSticky(id, stickyObject, data, value) {
		var campaignIds = [];

		campaignIds = id.split(',').map(function(item) {
			return item.trim();
		});

		if (!!~campaignIds.indexOf(String(data.campaignId))) {
			stickyObject = value;
		}

		return stickyObject;
	}

	window._isAdSizeReponsive = function(size) {
		for (var i = 0; i < window.responsiveAdSizes.length; i++) {
			if (
				window.responsiveAdSizes[i][0] === size[0] &&
				window.responsiveAdSizes[i][1] === size[1]
			) {
				return true;
			}
		}
		return false;
	};

	window._getSizeMapping = function(sizes) {
		var responsiveSizes = sizes.filter(_isAdSizeReponsive);
		var nonResponsiveSizes = sizes.filter(function(s) { return !_isAdSizeReponsive(s) });

		var sizeMapping = [{minWidth: 0}];

		var getItemIndex = function(arr, objKey, objVal) {
			for (var i; i < arr.length; i++) {
				if (arr[i][objKey] !== undefined && arr[i][objKey] === objVal) {
					return i;
				}
			}
			return -1;
		};

		sizeMapping = nonResponsiveSizes.reduce(function(mapping, size) {
			if (getItemIndex(mapping, 'minWidth', size[0]) < 0) {
				mapping.push({minWidth: size[0]});
			}
			return mapping;
		}, sizeMapping);

		sizeMapping = sizeMapping.map(function(map) {
			map.sizes = responsiveSizes
				.concat(
					nonResponsiveSizes.filter(function(size) {
						return size[0] <= map.minWidth;
					})
				)
				.sort(function(a, b) {
					if (a[0] === b[0]) {
						if (a[1] < b[1]) { return -1; }
						if (a[1] > b[1]) { return 1; }
					} else {
						if (a[0] < b[0]) { return -1; }
						if (a[0] > b[0]) { return 1; }
					}
					return 0;
				});
			return map;
		});

		var sorted = sizeMapping.sort(function(a, b) {
			if (a.minWidth < b.minWidth) { return -1; }
			if (a.minWidth > b.minWidth) { return 1; }
			return 0;
		});

		return sorted;
	};

	window._buildSizeMapping = function(sizeMapping) {
		var s = googletag.sizeMapping();
		for (var i = 0; i < sizeMapping.length; i++) {
			s.addSize([sizeMapping[i].minWidth, 0], sizeMapping[i].sizes);
		}
		return s.build();
	};

	window._defineAdSlot = function(unitSettings, positionContainerId) {
		var isPerfTest = getUrlParameter('perf_test') === '1';
		var adUnitName = unitSettings.unit;
		var unit = window.adUnits[adUnitName];
		var sizeMapping = _getSizeMapping(unit.sizes);

		adUnitName = unit.unitName !== undefined ? unit.unitName : unitSettings.unit;

		var slot = window.googletag
			.defineSlot(
				_dfpUnitPrefix + (isPerfTest ? 'hs-perf-test' : adUnitName),
				unit.sizes,
				positionContainerId
			);

		if (sizeMapping.length > 1) {
			slot.defineSizeMapping(
				_buildSizeMapping(sizeMapping)
			)
		}

		slot.addService(googletag.pubads());

		return slot;
	};

	window._defineAdPosition = function(positionId) {
		var adPosition = getAdPosition(positionId);
		if (!adPosition) return;

		if (typeof adPosition[window.adViewport] === "undefined") {
			return false;
		}

		var unitSettings = adPosition[window.adViewport];

		var slot = window._defineAdSlot(unitSettings, positionId);

		if (unitSettings.renderEnded !== undefined) {
			slot.renderEnded = unitSettings.renderEnded;

			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
				if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === positionId) {
					unitSettings.renderEnded(event);
					addCampaignIdToDataLayer(event);
				}
			});
		}

		if (unitSettings.onLoad !== undefined) {
			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotOnload', function(data) {
				if (slot === data.slot) {
					unitSettings.onLoad(data);
				}
			});
		}

		if (adPosition.collapseEmptyDiv !== undefined && adPosition.collapseEmptyDiv) {
			slot.setCollapseEmptyDiv(true);
		}

		adPosition.slot = slot;
	};

	window._displayAdPosition = function(positionId) {
		var adPosition = getAdPosition(positionId);
		if (!adPosition) return;

		if (typeof adPosition[window.adViewport] === "undefined") {
			return false;
		}

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.display(positionId);
			if (positionId === 'leaderboard-top') {
				// set ad iframe to width and height of zero
				// this is before ad data is loaded
				var ad = document.querySelector('#' + positionId + ' iframe');
				if (ad !== null) {
					ad.height = 0;
					ad.width = 0;
				}
			}
		});
	};

	window._initAdPosition = function(positionId) {
		var adPosition = getAdPosition(positionId);
		if (!adPosition) return;


		if (adPosition.lazy === undefined || !adPosition.lazy) {
			window._displayAdPosition(positionId);
		}

		const ad = document.querySelector(`#${positionId}`);
    if (ad) {
			ad.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
		}
	}

	googletag.cmd.push(function() {

		var pubadsService = googletag.pubads();

		for (var adPosKey in window.adPositions) {
			window._defineAdPosition(adPosKey);
		}

		
		pubadsService.setTargeting("env", "production");
		pubadsService.setTargeting("frontpage", "1");
		pubadsService.setTargeting("nsfw", "0");
		pubadsService.setTargeting("adult_content", "0");

		if (customTargetingValue) {
